0x002352b2 Long Sword: 1m long. Essential in monster caves.

0x002352f4 Falsion: Large steel sword. Good attack power.

0x00235336 Flame Sword: Fire blade. Easy use and lethal.

0x00235378 Light Saber: Strongest sword in existence.

0x002353a8 Fire Magic: Rapid fire. Works anywhere.

0x002353ea Fire DX: Fire magic splits into 3.

0x00235442 Homing: 6 shots chase foes. Some immune.

0x00235484 Force: Fire own magic energy at foes.

0x002354e0 Tail Attack: Spin and tail deal huge damage.

0x00235522 Ax: Powerful weapon. Slices foes in half.

0x00235582 Firebreath: Release stored power. Huge power.

0x002355bc Leather Mail: Layered horse leather. Low defense.

0x002355fe Chain Mail: Woven chains. Durable. Useful.

0x00235640 Plate Mail: Heavy steel. Fights off some attacks.

0x00235682 Silver Mail: Needed to fight many enemies.

0x002852ec Long Sword: 1m long. Essential in monster caves.

0x0028547c Homing: 6 shots chase foes. Some immune.

0x0028551a Tail Attack: Spin and tail deal huge damage.

0x0028555c Ax: Powerful weapon. Slices foes in half.
